Platinum Certified Super High Efficiency</li>    <li>DC Connector Panel with Integrated VRM (Voltage Regulator Module)</li>    <li>DC to DC Converter Design</li>    <li>Dual Copper Bars</li>    <li>Active Power Factor Correction (99% PF Typical)</li>    <li>Conductive Polymer Aluminum Solid Capacitors</li>    <li>Highly Reliable 105&deg;C Japanese Aluminum Electrolytic Capacitors</li>    <li>Gold Plated High Current Terminals</li>    <li>Ultra Tight Voltage Regulation </li>    <li>High +12V Output</li>    <li>Dual Sided PCB Layout</li>    <li>Seasonic Patented Hybrid Silent Fan Control</li>    <li>Sanyo Denki San Ace Silent Fan</li>    <li>Ultra Ventilation (Honeycomb Structure)</li>    <li>Full Modular Cabling Design</li>    <li>Multi-GPU Technology Support</li>    <li>All-in-One DC Cabling Design</li>    <li>Easy Swap Connector</li>    <li>Universal AC Input (Full Range)</li>   </ul>   <br />   <br style="clear:both;">  </div>  <div class="features l-staggered">   <h2 class="title">Special Features </h2>   <div class="features-block">    <img class="l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/17/151/17-151-140/i1.jpg" alt="SeaSonic Power Supply">    <p> <strong>Ultra Tight Voltage Regulation</strong> <br> Improved load voltage regulation keeps the voltage fluctuations on the 12V output within +2% and 0% (no negative tolerance), and on the 3.3V and 5V outputs between +1% and -1%, which (under 80 PLUS load conditions) results in smooth and stable operation. </p>    <br style="clear:both;">   </div>   <hr />   <div class="features-block">    <img class="l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/17/151/17-151-140/i2.jpg" alt="SeaSonic Power Supply">    <p> <strong>Seasonic Hybrid Silent Fan Control - S&sup2;FC & S&sup3;FC *</strong> <br> The industry first, advanced three-phased thermal control balances between silence and cooling. The Hybrid Silent Fan Control provides three operational stages: Fanless, Silent, and Cooling Mode. In addition, there is a switch provided to allow for manual selection between the Seasonic S&sup2;FC (fan control without Fanless Mode) and the S&sup3;FC (fan control including Fanless Mode). </p>    <br style="clear:both;">   </div>   <hr /><br />   <div class="l-center"> <img class="l-center" style="margin-bottom:10px;" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/17/151/17-151-140/i4.jpg" alt="SeaSonic Power Supply"></div>   <p><strong>Benefits:</strong></p>   <ul>    <li>Reduces noise without increasing temperature.</li>    <li>Extends fan life by eliminating unnecessary rotation.</li>    <li>Optimizes heat dissipation at all times.</li>    <li>Fanless Mode provides unsurpassed silent performance.</li>   </ul>   <p><strong>New Feature:</strong> Hysteresis is achieved by a fan control IC, which optimizes how frequently the fan switches on and off. At 25 &deg;C ambient temperature the fan turns on when the load rises above 35% (&plusmn; 5%) and it turns off when the load drops below 25% (&plusmn; 5%). Due to this lag in response the fan switches on and off less frequently, which reduces power loss in Fanless and Silent Mode. </p>   <hr />   <br />   <div class="features-block">    <img class="l-left" src="http://c1.neweggimages.com/BizIntell/item/17/151/17-151-140/i3.jpg" alt="SeaSonic Power Supply"> <br />    <p> <strong>Dual Copper Bars</strong> <br> These pure copper bars conduct high current more efficiently to reduce impedance and minimize voltage drop. </p>    <br style="clear:both;">   </div>  </div>  <div class="specifications bottBord">   <h2 class="title">Product Information</h2>   <br />   <div class="l-center">    <table>     <tr>      <td>DC Output Voltage</td>      <td>+3.3V</td>      <td>+5V</td>      <td>+12V</td>      <td>-12V</td>      <td>+5Vsb</td>     </tr>     <tr>      <td>Maximum Load</td>      <td>25A</td>      <td>25A</td>      <td>100A</td>      <td>0.5A</td>      <td>3A</td>     </tr>     <tr>      <td>Combined Load</td>      <td
